 Often people eat more food when they are hungry, but health experts say that people often eat more food even in stress situations
 haalanki aisa karne waalon kii sankhya bahut kam he
 According to catering experts, excessive eating is a disease and can occur under any circumstance
 aksar tanaav kii sthiti main, lambey samay tak bhookha rahane ke kaaran or khanpan ke kai vikalp uplabdh rahane kii sthiti main log atyadhik bhojan kar lete hai
 Health experts recommend keeping a check on food habits, saying that overeating can harm health
 atyadhik khanpan ke kaarnon kaa zikr karte hue diatician akshita agarwal ne kaha, 'aam taur par jab log bhavuk yaa tanaav main hote hai to ve adhik bhojan karte hai
 Sometimes due to the long interval between two meals, people eat more at one time
 'agarwal ke mutabik, saamaanya se adhik teji se khaanaa atyadhik bhojan karne kaa ek lakshan he
 He said that due to overeating, the percentage of body fat can increase and indigestion and stomach problems can occur
 mahilaon main hormone sambandhi asantulan bhi paidaa ho saktaa he, jisase masik dharm main aniyamitata aa sakati he or bal girnaa shuru ho saktaa he
 Divya Chaudhary, chief dietician at Max Hospital in Shalimar Bagh, also said, 'some people eat more food during stressful days and some eat less
 isaki vajah se logon main bal girane, calcium kii kami, pratirohak kshamta main kami, chehre par chamak main kami tathaa anemia kii shikaayat ho jaati he
 He said that excessive eating leads to weight gain and can lead to many medical complications
 haalanki maansarovar garden main dow
 Dietician Pawan Sethi in Rachnaz Diet says that the percentage of people who eat more during stressful days is less
 unhone kaha, 'aajkal log kaamkaaj ke silsile main jaldi ghar se nikal jate hai or isliye naashtaa nahin kar pate
 Whenever they get time to eat, they eat more food

 shabd jab yatra par nikal paden to jo kahani nikalati he vah kamare or vichaar se aage khurduri jameen kaa sach hoti he
 Where life smells and smells of concern
 lekin yatra karte vakt jehan main ubharate shabd yaa vichaaron ko pankh detii ankhen jab kaagaj par kuch ukerti hai to ve sirf safar kii kahani nahin kahatee balki lekhak ke jivan ke safar kaa hissaa ban jaati hai
 Here the writer breaks his own box which he has made with his understanding, his concern and his surroundings
 shaayad isiilie teen yatra vrittanton ko teen alag-alag parivesh se nikle yatri lekhakon ko ek saath khadaa karne kaa majaa hi kuch or he
 And if there is more travel than the writer in this line of writers, then the matter is different
 khaskar desh ke un ilaakon kii yatra jahaan kaa naam lete hi pathak ke jehan main tarah-tarah ke parivesh aa khadey hote hai
 If writer Asghar Wajahat travels from Azerbaijan to Port Blair and from Konkan to Shimoga in search of a path, litterateur Pankaj Bisht if he goes through the library documents in search of his country, slips through the mountains of Uttarakhand, along with life and ideology in Gujarat Including the speed of changing social stagnation in four decades, it is a different fun
 or yuva patrkaar anil yadav vakt or muflisi ko aainaa dikhaane ke liye uttar-purv ke ek aise safar par nikalen jahaan jindagi kaa matlab he jaddojahad, jahaan jivan kaa matlab he do june kii roti
 Where comfort means failure, then in such a situation it comes to say that there is some descent, too! So three accounts together
 lekin teenon kaa najariya alag-alag
 The process of traveling, seeing and experiencing it varies
 yatra ko lekhan kii style main utaarne kaa tarika alag-alag
 It is difficult, but for profit, when a publisher takes this trouble and prints all the three travel accounts together, then the reader should also risk reading the yatra from a new perspective
 patrkaar anil yadav kii yatra uttar purv ke us sach ko tatolane kaa prayaas he, jahaan kii yatra ke dauraan lekhak kii apni kam mushkilen nahin hai
 If a writer hides his difficulties often, then he wants to highlight the same atmosphere with the same difficulties, where it seems that the journey is indeed the reader
 asagar vajahat taxi, bas or taange se lekar alag-alag saamaajik parivesh se kuch is tarah ru-ba-rou karaate hai, jisamen lekhak ke shabdon ke saath padhane vaale ko bhi mahasoos hota he ki vah bhi safar kar rahaa he
 Here he realizes that Asgar Vajahat has a pen in his journey
 lekin anil yadav ke saath safar main pathak thakegaa, haanphega, traasadee bhogega or phir gusse main aise safar ko na karne kii hidaayat bhi degaa
 But then the reader will make the mistake of considering himself as a writer, not from the perspective of travel but from the perspective of compulsion to travel
 yahaan yadav kaa patrakaariya paksh haaavee hota he
 Readers will really enjoy examining that on one hand the journey to Wajahat, which is relaxed with information, which borrows the authoritative 'male' by causing discomfort to travel
 duusari ore, yadav luhaar kii tarah yatra ko peet-petakar vrittant banaate hai kyonki yatra sukun nahin he
 This is both pain and tragedy
 pankaj bisht ke likhe hue main uttarakhand ke jangalon ke khatm hone main sarkaar ke jangalraj kaa bodh hota he
 In Gujarat, they see that in Dwarka, the condition of testing the people of religion was hung on the door of the temple itself
 safar ke jariye desh ke sach ko ukerte in teenon hi lekhakon kaa vaasta kahin na kahin uttar-puvir rajya ke un logon se padataa hi he, jahaan bahut-se log aaj bhi bharat ko ek alag desh ke taur par dekhte hai
 In the midst of all this, through these three books, readers can also find the answer to that question, where it is said that the writer-writer-journalist captures the pulse
 yaa phir ab is daur main in logon ke sarokaar bache hi nahin hai, yaa unka lekhan unheen kii swayambhu jaankaree kaa gulam ho chukaa he
 Believe it, through the three authors of these three books, you really start thinking about literature and writing, that this is a journey started in the search of which path
 aapako yah bhi lag saktaa he ki yah kaisaa desh he
 Or maybe, after reading these three books, you also really cut the ticket and say, every time, the thought of turning the house, o wish! Would have gone a long way
 maujuuda samay main bhartiya cricket team kaa pradarshan ausat se behatar nahin ho paa rahaa he
 The team finds a solution to one problem and loses due to another problem
 ballebaaz behatar karte hai to gendbaaz team ko duubo dete hai
 When the bowlers do better, the batting falls apart
 captain mahendra singh dhoni kii captaini lagaataar sawaalon ke ghere main hai
 Dhoni, once known as 'captain Cool', appears to be a club level captain
 kehete hai ki jab pradarshan lagaataar kharaab ho to aatmavishvaas dagamagane lagata he
 Team India has also become a staggering boat right now
 in tamaam mushkilon ke bich hi he number saat kaa sankat

 maujuuda team ke paas aisa koi upyogi khilaadi nahin dikh rahaa he

 team ke captain mahendra singh dhoni ke out hone ke baad jadeja ko wicket par tikna tha lekin vah jaldi hi pavilion laut gaye
 Jadeja's performance has been average since his return to Team India
 beete teen vanade maichon main jadeja ne 727 or 13 kaa score banaaya he

 unhone mahaj 10 din ke andar do−do tihare shatak jamaaye hai
